2003-05-23: nuncanada@h0ly.: ChangeSet 1.846.1.23
  Making xarVarPrepForOS checks saner. Added wildcards '?' and '*' to them, although i dont know if there could be a use case with these? 
  	* html/includes/xarVar.php:
	  Chaging the check for something more sane in the xarPrepForOS Changed from preg_replace to strtr. Changed what is looked for, to hit special characters not only special cases. A major vulnerability in PHP scripts out there is because it doesnt properly check the name of the file, most of the time you can pass something like hack.php\ thru the system with a little POST hacking to get this name there. As the scripts usually check for .php ending, .php\ pass thru, and the OS ends up saving this as 'hack.php'
